<review>I am buying into Wallis Ranch this spring. While I can understand all the negative and positive reviews on here, our purchase was decided based on our personal lifestyle.

We currently own another home with a front lawn and back yard. With lots of money spent landscaping then maintaining, we are done with it. Our home is older home so we've always had to deal with upgrades, remodeling and maintenance. Again, we're done with that.

Wallis Ranch suited our lifestyle. We bought a 3000sf home for the same price as other existing smaller homes in Dublin. We love the kindred house and it's amenities. We love the fact that the community is secured and gated. We also like the fact that shopping, grocery, restaurants, golf etc are close by.

For us, we bought into a new home, convenience, amenities and not to mention, great schools. The community works perfect for US.

If you're looking for a newer home with more land and lower priced, move to Sacramento or Lodi or Bakersfield or Las Vegas. It just doesn't exist here in the Bay Area.< /review>< user_name>
Jason Pugao< /user_name>

I decided to move to Wallis ranch because it's a gated community, close proximity to everything, and the kindred house. For the HOA fee versus what you get. It's really cheap. <Text>The best thing about these¬†restaurants, verging on an affectionately accepted foible, is that they‚Äôre always out of something on the menu. This was true at three of the four places I visited, but they had everything I asked for at this hot, smoky fun cranny, colorfully decorated with the flags of the region and the requisite portrait of Bob Marley. Admittedly, I went for lunch, and kept my order simple: chicken tacos ($9.95) and a beef burritos ($12.78).
